                <i class="quality-layer-arrow-r"></i>
                <div>
                    <p>新车百车故障数=参与评价的新车发生的故障数÷参与评价的新车数×100</p>
                    <p>表示平均每百辆新车中出现的故障数，包含故障、异响、使用不便等问题。新车百车故障数值越小，代表质量越好。</p>

            <!-- 二手车保值率入口浮层开始 -->
           <div class="quality-layer-chexi pop pop-left fn-hide" id="preservation-layer-chexi" style="visibility: visible; top: 1313.5px; left: 96.4531px;">
              <i class="quality-layer-arrow-r"></i>
              <div>
                <h2>什么是保值率?</h2>
                <p>汽车保值率又称残值，是指车辆在使用几年后，将其卖出的价格与新车价格的比值。</p>
                <p>新车购买使用几年后，在市场上的出售价格处以该车新车的指导价，得出来的百分比比值就是保值率。</p>
                <p>保值率越高，该车的二手车在市场上就越值钱。</p>
              </div>
            </div>
        </div>

            var myurl = "//dealer.api.autohome.com.cn/dealerrest/Profile/GetRecommendDealers?_appid=cms&_seriesId=" + seriesid + "&cityId=" + SeriesCityId + "&_rowCount=2";
            $.ajax({
                url: myurl ,
                type:'get',
                dataType: 'jsonp',
                cache: true,
                jsonp: '_callback',
                jsonpCallback: 'isdealer',
                scriptCharset:'utf-8',
                success: function(data) 
                {
                    if (data.returncode > 0 || data.message != "" || !data.result || data.result.rowcount == 0) {
                        return
                    }
                    var dealerhtml = "";
                    for (var i = 0; i < data.result.list.length; i++) {
                        if (!document.getElementById("ad_word_0" + (i + 1))) continue;
                        dealerhtml = tempHtml;
                        if (!data.result.list[i].IsDealer) dealerhtml = dealerhtml.replace("{Title}",  '<a href="'+data.result.list[i].LinkUrl+'">'+data.result.list[i].Company+'</a>');
                        else dealerhtml = dealerhtml.replace("{Title}", '<a href="//dealer.autohome.com.cn/{DealerId}/#pvareaid={PvId}">{DealerName}</a>');
                        dealerhtml = dealerhtml.replace("{DealerId}", data.result.list[i].DealerId);
                        dealerhtml = dealerhtml.replace("{DealerName}", data.result.list[i].Company);
                        dealerhtml = dealerhtml.replace("{StyledPhone}", data.result.list[i].AsSellPhone);
                        switch (i) {
                            case 0:
                                dealerhtml = dealerhtml.replace("{PvId}", 101546);
                                break;
                            case 1:
                                dealerhtml = dealerhtml.replace("{PvId}", 101547);
                                break
                        }
                        document.getElementById("ad_word_0" + (i + 1)).innerHTML = dealerhtml
                    }
                    DealerResAdmin.resLoader('ad_word_01', '10000', SeriesCityId, seriesid, 0,false);
                    return;
                }
            })

            $(function() {
                var scrollFloat = function(id) {
                    var $elem = $(id),
                    $temp,
                    $nav,
                    create = function() {
                        $temp = $('<div style="width:' + (sup.fixed ? $elem.width() : "1000") + 'px;margin:0 auto;height:0;display:none;"><div id="_tempscrollFloat" class="' + $elem[0].className + '" style="z-index:1000;top:0;height:' + $elem.height() + "px;width:" + $elem.width() + "px;position:" + (sup.fixed ? "fixed": "absolute") + ";" + $elem[0].style.cssText + '">' + $elem.html() + "</div></div>");
                        $temp.appendTo("body");
                        $nav = $temp.children("div")
                    },
                    set = function() {
                        var wT = $(window).scrollTop(),
                        pos = $elem.offset();
                        if (wT > pos.top) {
                            if (sup.fixed) {
                                $temp.show()
                            } else {
                                $nav.css("top", wT + "px");
                                $temp.show()
                            }
                        } else {
                            $temp.hide()
                        }
                    };
                    create();
                    set();
                    $(window).on("scroll resize", set)
                };

                WindowScroll();
                function WindowScroll(){
                    var thisButtomTop = parseInt($(window).height()) + parseInt($(window).scrollTop());  
                    var thisTop = parseInt($(window).scrollTop()); 
                    if($(".financial").length>0){
                        var PictureTop = parseInt($(".financial").offset().top);  
                        if (PictureTop >= thisTop && PictureTop <= thisButtomTop) {
                            if($('.financial #tab3-1 div.series-financial').html()==""&&ScrollLock){
                                ScrollLock=false;
                                autoseries.financial(seriesid,auto.area.cityId,'index');
                            }

            $('[data-type="spec-attention"]').each(function(index, item) {
                attentionspecList.push($(item).attr("data-specid"));
            });
            if(attentionspecList.length>0){
                $.ajax({
                    url: '//dealer.api.autohome.com.cn/buyapi/spec/GetSpecMinPriceByCity?_appId=cms&specIds='+attentionspecList.join(',')+'&cityid=' + SeriesCityId,
                    type: 'get',
                    dataType: 'jsonp',
                    jsonp: '_callback',
                    jsonpCallback: 'DealerBySpecRank',
                    cache: true,
                    success: function (data) {
                        try {
                            var isshowspec=false;
                            if (data.returncode == 0 && data.result != undefined && data.result.list != undefined && data.result.list.length > 0) {
                                for (var i = 0; i < data.result.list.length; i++) {
                                    if(data.result.list[i].PriceOff>0){
                                        var items=$('[data-specid="'+data.result.list[i].SpecId+'"]');
                                        items.html('<a href="'+data.result.list[i].LinkUrl+'#pvareaid="><i class="icon12 icon12-down"></i>'+ Math.round((data.result.list[i].PriceOff / 10000) * 100) / 100.00+'万</a>');
                                        items.next().html(Math.round((data.result.list[i].Price / 10000) * 100) / 100.00+"万起");
                                        $("#JJ_"+data.result.list[i].SpecId).attr("PriceOff",data.result.list[i].PriceOff).show();
                                        isshowspec=true;
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                            if(isshowspec){
                                var arr=  $('.uibox-con.price-off-wrap ul li').get();
                                arr.sort(function(a, b) {
                                    var ai = parseFloat($(a).attr("PriceOff"), 10);
                                    var bi = parseFloat($(b).attr("PriceOff"), 10);
                                    if (ai > bi) {
                                        return -1;
                                    } else if (ai < bi) {
                                        return 1;
                                    } else {
                                        return 0;
                                    }
                                });
                                $('.uibox-con.price-off-wrap ul').append(arr);
                                $('.uibox-con.price-off-wrap').parent().show();
                                $('div[class="price-off-item"]').each(function(index, item) {
                                    if(index == 0){
                                        $(item).prepend("<i class='rank-icon rank-first'>"+(index+1)+"</i>"); 
                                    }else{
                                        $(item).prepend("<i class='rank-icon'>"+(index+1)+"</i>"); 
                                    }
                                
                                    $(item).find("p:eq(0)").find("a").attr('href',$(item).find("p:eq(0)").find("a").attr("href").replace("#pvareaid=","#pvareaid=20232"+(index+index+78)));
                                    $(item).find("p:eq(1)").find("a").attr('href',$(item).find("p:eq(1)").find("a").attr("href").replace("#pvareaid=","#pvareaid=20232"+(index+index+78)));
                                    if($(item).find("p:eq(2)").find("a").attr("href")!=undefined){
                                        $(item).find("p:eq(2)").find("a").attr('href',$(item).find("p:eq(2)").find("a").attr("href").replace("#pvareaid=","#pvareaid=20232"+(index+index+79)));}
                                });
                            }
                        } catch (e) {}
                    }
                })
            }
            //二手车
            var isloadInterested=true;
            function loadInterested() {
                isloadInterested=false;
                $.ajax({
                    url: "//api.che168.com/auto/forautoserieschannel_v3_1.ashx",
                    data: {
                        '_appid': 'autoseries',
                        'cid': auto.area.cityId,
                        'sid': 3457 ,
                        'minprice': 14.59 ,
                        'maxprice': 22.89 ,
                        'topNum': 12
                    },
                    dataType: 'jsonp',
                    callback: 'callback',
                    jsonpCallback: 'che168InterestedCallback',
                    cache: true,
                    success: function(data) {
                        if (data.returncode != 0 || !data.result.carlist || data.result.carlist.length < 3) {
                            //$('#che168_price').hide();
                            return
                        }
                        $("#tab_1uibox").show();
                        isLoaded1 = true;
                        var point = 0;
                        if (data.result.carlist.length >= 1 && data.result.carlist.length <= 4) {
                            point = 1
                        } else if (data.result.carlist.length > 4 && data.result.carlist.length <= 8) {
                            point = 2
                        } else {
                            point = 3
                        }
                        for (var i = 0; i < point; i++) {
                            data.result.carlistorder = data.result.carlist.slice(i * 4, i * 4 + 4);
                            data.result.interest=true;
                            $('#che168_tab01').append($('#auto-series-2sc-tmpl-main').tmpl(data.result));
                            $('#che168_point01').append('<span' + (i == 0 ? ' class="selected"' : '') + '><a target="_self" href="javascript:void(0);"></a></span>')
                        }
                        $('#che168_province').append($('#auto-series-2sc-tmpl-city').tmpl(data.result.arealink));
                        $('#che168_areaurl').attr('href', data.result.areaurl);
                        $('#che168_gotoche168').attr('href', data.result.gotoche168);
                        $("#tab-11").focus();
                    }
                });
            }

            function loadSameSeries() {
                isloadSameSeries=false;
                $.ajax({
                    url: "//api.che168.com/auto/forautoserieschannel_v3_2.ashx",
                    data: {
                        '_appid': 'autoseries',
                        'cid': auto.area.cityId,
                        'sid': 3457 ,
                        'topNum': 12
                    },
                    dataType: 'jsonp',
                    callback: 'callback',
                    jsonpCallback: 'che168SameSeriesCallback',
                    cache: true,
                    success: function(data) {
                        isLoaded2 = true;
                        if (data.returncode != 0 || !data.result.carlist || data.result.carlist.length < 3) {
                            //$('#che168_tab12').hide();
                            //$('#tab-12').hide();
                            return
                        }
                        $("#tab_2uibox").show(); 
                        var num = 0,
                            point = 0;
                        if (data.result.carlist.length >= 1 && data.result.carlist.length <= 4) num = 4, point = 1;
                        else if (data.result.carlist.length > 4 && data.result.carlist.length <= 8) num = 8, point = 2;
                        else num = 12, point = 3;
                        //var dataCarList = [];
                        //for (var i = 0; i < num; i++) {
                        //    var item = data.result.carlist[i];
                        //    item.seriesname = autoAddEllipsis(item.carname, 16);
                        //    dataCarList.push(item)
                        //}
                        for (var i = 0; i < point; i++) {
                            data.result.carlistorder = data.result.carlist.slice(i * 4, i * 4 + 4);
                            data.result.interest=false;
                            $('#che168_tab02').append($('#auto-series-2sc-tmpl-main').tmpl(data.result));
                            $('#che168_point02').append('<span' + (i == 0 ? ' class="selected"' : '') + '><a target="_self" href="javascript:void(0);"></a></span>');
                        }
                        $('#che168_province2').append($('#auto-series-2sc-tmpl-city').tmpl(data.result.arealink));
                        $('#che168_areaurl2').attr('href', data.result.areaurl);
                        $('#che168_gotoche1682').attr('href', data.result.gotoche168);
                        $("#tab-12").focus();
                    }
                })
            }
